[30;1m60 | [0m[35m-   Provides an interface comparable to Python's builtin in `fnmatch`, `glob`, and `pathlib`.[0m
[30;1m61 | [0m[35m-   Allows for a much more configurable experience when matching or globbing with many more features[0m
[30;1m62 | [0m[35m-   Adds support for `**` in glob.[0m
[30;1m63 | [0m[35m-   Adds support for Zsh style `***` recursive glob for symlinks.[0m
[30;1m64 | [0m[35m-   Adds support for escaping characters with `\`.[0m
[30;1m65 | [0m[35m-   Add support for POSIX style character classes inside sequences: `[[:alnum:]]`, etc. The `C` loca[0m
[30;1m66 | [0m[35m-   Adds support for brace expansion: `a{b,{c,d}}` --> `ab ac ad`.[0m
